   Abhidharmasamuccaya	ABiDarma-samuccaya
   namo buddhāya	namaH budDAya
   [atha mūlavastuni tridharmaparicchedaḥ prathamaḥ /]	[aTa mUlavastuni triDarma-paricCedaH praTamaH /]
   tridharmaḥ saṃgrahaḥ saṃprayogo 'nvayaśca lakṣaṇe /	tri-DarmaH saMgrahaH saMprayogaH anvayaH-ca lakzaNe /
   viniścaye satyadharmau prāptiḥ sāṃkathyameva ca //	viniScaye satya-DarmO prAptiH sAMkaTyam-eva ca //
   kati kasmādupādānaṃ vyavasthānaṃ ca lakṣaṇam /	kati kasmAt-upAdAnam vyavasTAnam ca lakzaNam /
   anukamārthadṛṣṭāntabhedā jñeyāḥ samuccaye //	anukama-arTa-dRzwAnta-BedAH jQeyAH samuccaye //
   skandhā dhātava āyatanāni ca kati / skandhāḥ pañca / rūpaskandho	skanDAH DAtavaH AyatanAni ca kati / skanDAH paQca / rUpa-skanDaH-
   vedanāskandhaḥ saṃjñāskandhaḥ saṃskāraskandho vijñānaskandhaśca // dhātavo	vedanA-skanDaH saMjQA-skanDaH saMskAra-skanDaH vijQAna-skanDaH-ca // DAtavaH-
   'ṣṭādaśa / cakṣurdhātū rūpadhātuścakṣurvijñānadhātuḥ śrotradhātuḥ	azwAdaSa / cakzuH-DAtuH rUpa-DAtuH-cakzuH-vijQAna-DAtuH Srotra-DAtuH
   śabdadhātuḥ	Sabda-DAtuH
   śrotravijñānadhāturghrāṇadhāturgandhadhāturghrāṇavijñānadhāturjivhādhātū	Srotra-vijQAna-DAtuH-GrANa-DAtuH-ganDa-DAtuH-GrANa-vijQAna-DAtuH-jivhADAtU
   rasadhāturjivhāvijñānadhātuḥ kāyadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyadhātuḥ	rasa-DAtuH-jivhA-vijQAna-DAtuH kAyaDAtuH sprazwavya-DAtuH
   kāyavijñānadhāturmanodhāturdharmadhāturmanovijñānadhātuśca // āyatanāni	kAya-vijQAna-DAtuH-manaH-DAtuH-DarmaDAtuH-manaH-vijQAna-DAtuH-ca // AyatanAni
   dvadaśa / cakṣurāyatanaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ śrotrāyatanaṃ śabdāyatanaṃ	dvadaSa / cakzuH-Ayatanam rUpa-Ayatanam Srotra-Ayatanam Sabda-Ayatanam
   ghrāṇāyatanaṃ gandhāyatanaṃ jivhāyatanaṃ rasāyatanaṃ kāyāyatanaṃ	GrANa-Ayatanam ganDa-Ayatanam jivhA-Ayatanam rasa-Ayatanam kAya-Ayatanam
   spraṣṭavyāyatanaṃ manaāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanaṃ ca //	sprazwavya-Ayatanam manaA-Ayatanam Darma-Ayatanam ca //
   kimupādāya skandhāḥ pañcaiva / paṃcākārātmavastūdbhāvanatāmupādāya /	kim-upAdAya skanDAH paQca-eva / paMca-AkAra-Atma-vastu-udBAvana-tAm-upAdAya /
   saparigrahadehātmavastu upabhogātmavastu abhilāpātmavastu	sa-parigraha-deha-AtmavaH-tu upaBoga-Atmavastu aBilApa-Atma-vastu
   sarvadharmādharmābhisaṃskārātmavastu (Abhidh-s 2) tadāśrayātmasvastu	sarva-Darma-aDarma-aBisaMskAra-Atma-vastu (a-aBiD-H 2) tad-ASraya-Atma-svastu
   copādāya // kimupādāya dhātovo 'ṣṭādaśaiva / dvābhyāṃ	ca-upAdAya // kim-upAdAya DAtovaH azwAdaSa-eva / dvAByAm
   dehaparigrahābhyāmatītavarttamānaṣaḍākāropabhogadhāraṇatāmupādāya //	deha-parigrahAByAm-atIta-varttamAna-zaxa-AkAra-upaBoga-DAraNa-tAm-upAdAya //
   kimupādāyāyatanāni dvādaśaiva / dvābhyāṃ	kim-upAdAya-AyatanAni dvAdaSa-eva / dvAByAm
   dehaparigrahābhyāmanāgataṣaḍākāropabhogāyadvāratāmupādāya //	deha-parigrahAByAm-anAgata-zaxa-AkAra-upaBogAya-dvAra-tAm-upAdAya //
   kasmāt skandhā upādānamityucyante / upādānena sahitatvāt skandhā upādānami	kasmAt skanDAH upAdAnam-iti-ucyante / upAdAnena sahita-tvAt skanDAH upAdAnam-i
   tyucyante / upādānaṃ katamat / skandheṣu cchando rāgaśca / kasmāt /	ti-ucyante / upAdAnam katamat / skanDezu cCandaH rAgaH-ca / kasmAt /
   ḥcchando rāgaścopādānamityucyate /	HcCandaH rAgaH-ca-upAdAnam-iti-ucyate /
   anāgatavarttamānaskandhānāmabhinirvarttanato 'parihārataśca / anāgate	anAgata-varttamAna-skanDAnAm-aBinirvarttanataH aparihArataH-ca / anAgate
   'bhilāṣād varttamāne 'dhāvasānācca cchando rāgaścopādānamityucyate /	aBilAzAt varttamAne aDAvasAnAt-ca cCandaH rAgaH-ca-upAdAnam-iti-ucyate /
   kasmād dhātava āyatanāni ca sopādānadharmā ityucyante / tatra	kasmAt DAtavaH AyatanAni ca sa-upAdAna-DarmAH iti-ucyante / tatra
   skandhavannirddeśaḥ //	skanDa-vat-nirddeSaH //
   kiṃlakṣaṇaṃ rūpam / rūpaṇa lakṣaṇaṃ rūpam / tad dvividham / sparśena	kiMlakzaNam rUpam / rUpaNa lakzaNam rUpam / tat dviviDam / sparSena
   rūpaṇaṃ pradeśena rūpaṇaṃ ca / sparśena rūpaṇaṃ katamat /	rUpaNam pradeSena rUpaNam ca / sparSena rUpaNam katamat /
   karacaraṇapāṣāṇaśasradaṇḍaśītoṣṇakṣutpipāsāmaśakadaṃśasarpavṛścikādīnāṃ	kara-caraNa-pAzANa-Sasra-daNxa-SIta-uzNa-kzuD-pipAsA-maSaka-daMSa-sarpa-vRScika-AdInAm
   sparśena vyābādhanam / pradeśena rūpaṇaṃ katamat / deśena rūpaṇa midaṃ	sparSena vyAbADanam / pradeSena rUpaNam katamat / deSena rUpaNa midam
   cedaṃ ca rūpamevaṃ caivaṃ ca rūpamiti praṇihitāpraṇihitacetovitarkeṇa	ca-idam ca rUpam-evam ca-evam ca rUpam-iti praNihita-apraNihita-cetaH-vitarkeNa
   pratibimbacitrīkāratā // kiṃlakṣaṇā vedanā / anubhavalakṣaṇā vedanā /	pratibimba-citrIkAra-tA // kiMlakzaNA vedanA / anuBava-lakzaNA vedanA /
   nānāvidhānāṃ śubhaśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalavipākaṃ	nAnAviDAnAm SuBa-SuBAnAm karmaNAm Pala-vipAkam
   pratyanubhavantyanenetyanubhavaḥ // kiṃlakṣaṇā saṃjñā / saṃjānanālakṣaṇā	pratyanuBavanti-anena-iti-anuBavaH // kiMlakzaNA saMjQA / saMjAnanA-lakzaNA
   saṃjñā / saṃjñā nānādharmapratibimbodgrahaṇa (svabhāvā) yayā	saMjQA / saMjQA nAnA-Darma-pratibimba-udgrahaNa (svaBAvA) yayA
   draṣṭaśrutamatavijñātānarthān vyavaharati // kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ /	drazwa-Sruta-mata-vijQAtAn-arTAn vyavaharati // kiMlakzaNaH saMskAraH /
   abhisaṃskāralakṣaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ / saṃskārabhisaṃskāra (svabhāvo) yena	aBisaMskAra-lakzaNaH saMskAraH / saMskAra-BisaMskAraH (svaBAvo) yena
   kuśalākuśalāvyakṛteṣu pakṣeṣu cittaṃ prerayati / kiṃlakṣaṇaṃ (Abhidh-s 3)	kuSala-akuSalAvya-kRtezu pakzezu cittam prerayati / kiMlakzaNam (a-aBiD-H 3)
   vijñānam / vijānanālakṣaṇaṃ vijñānam / vijñānaṃ yena	vijQAnam / vijAnana-alakzaNam vijQAnam / vijQAnam yena
   rūpaśabdagandharasasparśadharmān nānā viṣayān vijānāti //	rUpa-Sabda-ganDa-rasa-sparSa-DarmAn nAnA vizayAn vijAnAti //
   cakṣurdhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ / yena cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭavān paśyati yacca	cakzuH-DAtuH kiMlakzaNaH / yena cakzuzA rUpANi dRzwavAn paSyati yat-ca
   tasya bījamupacitamālayavijñānaṃ taccakṣuḥ // yathā cakṣurdhātulakṣaṇaṃ	tasya bIjam-upacitam-Alaya-vijQAnam tat-cakzuH // yaTA cakzuH-DAtu-lakzaNam
   tathā śrotraghrāṇajihyakāyamanodhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni / rūpadhātuḥ	taTA Srotra-GrANa-jihya-kAya-manaH-DAtUnAm-api lakzaNAni / rUpa-DAtuH
   kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ / rūpaṃ yaccakṣuṣā dṛṣṭaṃ dṛśyate ca yacca tatra	kiMlakzaNaH / rUpam yat-cakzuzA dRzwam dRSyate ca yat-ca tatra
   cakṣurdhātorādhipatyaṃ tadrūpadhātu lakṣaṇam / yathā rūpadhātu lakṣaṇaṃ	cakzuH-DAtoH-ADipatyam tad-rUpa-DAtu lakzaNam / yaTA rUpa-DAtu lakzaNam
   tathā śabdagandharasasparśadharmadhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni /	taTA Sabda-ganDa-rasa-sparSa-Darma-DAtUnAm-api lakzaNAni /
   cakṣūrvijñānadhātuḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ / cakṣurāśrayā rūpālambanā	cakzUH-vijQAna-DAtuH kiMlakzaNaH / cakzuH-ASrayA rUpa-AlambanA
   rūpaprativijñaptiḥ yacca tasya bījamupacitaṃ / vipākālayavijñānaṃ	rUpa-prativijQaptiH yat-ca tasya bIjam-upacitam / vipAka-Alaya-vijQAnam
   taccakṣurvijñānadhātulakṣaṇam // yathā cakṣurvijñānadhātulakṣaṇaṃ tathā	tad-cakzuH-vijQAna-DAtu-lakzaNam // yaTA cakzuH-vijQAna-DAtu-lakzaNam taTA
   śrotraghrāṇajivhākāyamanovijñānadhātūnāmapi lakṣaṇāni //	Srotra-GrANa-jivhA-kAya-manaH-vijQAna-DAtUnAm-api lakzaNAni //
   āyatanaṃ kiṃlakṣaṇam / dhātuvad yathāyogaṃ veditavyam //	Ayatanam kiMlakzaNam / DAtu-vat yaTAyogam veditavyam //
   rūpaskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat / yatkiṃcidrūpaṃ sarvaṃ taccatvāri	rUpa-skanDa-vyavasTAnam katamat / yat-kiMcid-rUpam sarvam tat-catvAri
   mahābhūtāni catvāri ca mahābhūtānyupādāya // katamāni catvāri mahābhūtāni	mahABUtAni catvAri ca mahABUtAni-upAdAya // katamAni catvAri mahABUtAni
   / pṛthivīdhātuḥ abdhātuḥ tejodhātuḥ vāyudhātuśca // pṛthivīdhātuḥ katamaḥ	/ pRTivI-DAtuH abDAtuH tejaH-DAtuH vAyuDAtuH-ca // pRTivI-DAtuH katamaH
   / kaṭhinatā // abdhātuḥ katamaḥ niṣyandatā // tejodhātuḥ katamaḥ / uṣṇatā	/ kaWina-tA // abDAtuH katamaH nizyandatA // tejaH-DAtuH katamaH / uzNa-tA
   // vāyudhātuḥ katamaḥ / kampanatā // upādāya rūpaṃ katamat /	// vAyuDAtuH katamaH / kampanatA // upAdAya rUpam katamat /
   cakṣurindriyaṃ śrotrendriyaṃ ghrāṇendriyaṃ jivhendriyaṃ kāyendriyaṃ	cakzuH-indriyam Srotra-indriyam GrANa-indriyam jivhA-indriyam kAya-indriyam
   rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyānāmekadeśo dharmāyatanasaṃgṛhītaṃ ca rūpam //	rUpa-Sabda-ganDa-rasa-sprazwavyAnAm-eka-deSaH Darma-Ayatana-saMgRhItam ca rUpam //
   cakṣurindriyaṃ katamat / catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya cakṣuvijñānā śrayo	cakzuH-indriyam katamat / catvAri mahABUtAni-upAdAya cakzu-vijQAnA SrayaH-
   rūpaprasādaḥ // śrotrendriyaṃ katamat / catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya	rUpa-prasAdaH // Srotra-indriyam katamat / catvAri mahABUtAni-upAdAya
   śrotravijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ / ghrāṇendriyaṃ katamat / catvāri	Srotra-vijQAna-ASrayaH rUpa-prasAdaH / GrANa-indriyam katamat / catvAri
   mahābhūtānyupādāya ghrāṇavijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ // jivhendriyaṃ katamat	mahABUtAni-upAdAya GrANa-vijQAna-ASrayaH rUpa-prasAdaH // jivha-indriyam katamat-
   / catvāri mahabhūtānyupādāya jivhāvijñānaśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ // kāyendriyaṃ	/ catvAri maha-BUtAni-upAdAya jivhA-vijQAna-SrayaH rUpa-prasAdaH // kAya-indriyam
   katamat / catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya kāyavijñānāśrayo rūpaprasādaḥ //	katamat / catvAri mahABUtAni-upAdAya kAya-vijQAna-ASrayaH rUpa-prasAdaH //
   rūpaṃ katamat / catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya cakṣurindriyagocaro 'rthaḥ /	rUpam katamat / catvAri mahABUtAni-upAdAya cakzuH-indriya-gocaraH arTaH /
   yathā nīlaṃ pītaṃ lohitamavadātaṃ dīrghaṃ hrasvaṃ vṛttaṃ parimaṇḍalaṃ	yaTA nIlam pItam lohitam-avadAtam dIrGam hrasvam vRttam parimaNxalam
   sthūlaṃ sūkṣmamunnatamavanataṃ sātaṃ visātamātapaḥ chāyā āloko	sTUlam sUkzmam-unnatam-avanatam sAtam visAtam-AtapaH CAyA AlokaH-
   'dhakāramabhraṃ dhūmo rajo mahikā ca / abhyavakāśarūpaṃ vijñaptirūpaṃ	aDakAram-aBram DUmaH rajaH mahikA ca / aByavakASa-rUpam vijQapti-rUpam
   nabha ekavarṇaṃ rūpam // tat (Abhidh-s 4) punastridhā /	naBaH eka-varNam rUpam // tat (a-aBiD-H 4) punar-triDA /
   śobhanamaśobhanamubhayaviparītaṃ ca // śabdaḥ katamaḥ / catvāri	SoBanam-aSoBanam-uBaya-viparItam ca // SabdaH katamaH / catvAri
   mahābhūtānyupādāya śrotrendriyabrāhyo 'rthaḥ / manojño vā amanojño vā	mahABUtAni-upAdAya Srotra-indriya-brAhyaH arTaH / manojQaH vA amanojQaH vA
   ubhayaviparīto vā / upāttamahābhūtahetuko vā anupāttamahābhūtahetuko vā	uBaya-viparItaH vA / upAtta-mahABUta-hetukaH vA anupAtta-mahABUta-hetukaH vA
   tadubhayo bālokaprasiddho vā siddhopanīto vā parikalpito vā āryairdeśito	tat-uBayaH bAloka-prasidDaH vA sidDa-upanItaH vA parikalpitaH vA AryEH-deSitaH-
   vā tīrthaidaśito vā / gandhaḥ katamaḥ / catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya	vA tIrTEdaSitaH vA / ganDaH katamaH / catvAri mahABUtAni-upAdAya
   ghrāṇendriyagrāhyo 'rthaḥ / yathā surabhirasurabhiḥ samagandhaḥ	GrANa-indriya-grAhyaH arTaH / yaTA suraBiH-asuraBiH sama-ganDaH
   sahajagandhaḥ sāṃyogikagandhaḥ pāriṇāmikagandhaśca // rasaḥ katama /	sahaja-ganDaH sAMyogika-ganDaH pAriNAmika-ganDaH-ca // rasaH katamaH /
   catvāri mahābhūtāmyupādāya jivhendriyabrāhyo 'rthaḥ / tikto 'mlo madhuraḥ	catvAri mahABUtAmi-upAdAya jivha-indriya-brAhyaH arTaH / tiktaH amlaH maDuraH
   kaṭuko lavaṇaḥ kaṣāyaśca / manojño vā amanojño vā ubhayaviparīto vā sahajo	kawukaH lavaNaH kazAyaH-ca / manojQaH vA amanojQaH vA uBaya-viparItaH vA sahajaH-
   vā sāṃyogiko vā pāriṇāmiko vā // spraṣṭavyaikadeśaḥ katamaḥ / catvāri	vA sAMyogikaH vA pAriNAmikaH vA // sprazwavya-eka-deSaH katamaH / catvAri
   mahābhūtānyupādāya kāyendriya grāhyo 'rthaḥ / ślakṣṇatvaṃ karkaśatvaṃ	mahABUtAni-upAdAya kAya-indriya grAhyaH arTaH / SlakzNa-tvam karkaSa-tvam
   laghutvaṃ gurūtvaṃ picchilatvaṃ mandatvamamandatvaṃ śītatvamuṣṇatvaṃ	laGu-tvam gurU-tvam picCila-tvam manda-tvam-amanda-tvam SIta-tvam-uzNa-tvam
   jighatsā pipāsā tṛptirbalaṃ daurbalayaṃ mūrcchā kaṇḍūtiḥ	jiGatsA pipAsA tRptiH-balam dOrbalayam mUrcCA kaNxUtiH
   pūtirvyādhirjarāmaraṇaṃ klāntirviśrāma ūrjā ca // dharmāyatanasaṃgṛhītaṃ	pUtiH-vyADiH-jarA-maraNam klAntiH-viSrAmaH UrjA ca // Darma-Ayatana-saMgRhItam
   rūpaṃ katamat / pañcavidham / ābhisaṃkṣepikamābhyavakāśiṃkaṃ sāmādānikaṃ	rUpam katamat / paQcaviDam / ABisaMkzepi-kam-AByavakA-SiMkam sAma-AdAnikam
   parikalpitaṃ vaibhutvikaṃ ca /	parikalpitam vEButvikam ca /
   vedanāskandhavyavasthānaṃ katamat / ṣaḍvedanākāyāḥ / cakṣuḥsaṃsparśajā	vedanA-skanDa-vyavasTAnam katamat / zaz-vedanA-kAyAH / cakzuH-saMsparSa-jA
   vedanā śrotraghrāṇajivhākāyamanaḥ saṃsparśajā vedanā // evaṃ ṣaḍvedanā	vedanA Srotra-GrANa-jivhAkA-yamanaH saMsparSa-jAH vedanA // evam zaz-vedanA
   kāyāḥ sukhā vā duḥkhā aduḥkhāsukhā vā // punaḥ sukhā kāyikī vedanā duḥkhā	kAyAH suKAH vA duHKAH aduHKa-asuKA vA // punar suKA kAyikI vedanA duHKA
   kāyikī vedanā aduḥkhāsukhā kāyikīvedanā sukhā caitasikī vedanā duḥkhā	kAyikI vedanA aduHKa-asuKA kAyikI-vedanA suKA cEtasikI vedanA duHKA
   caitasikī vedanā aduḥkhāsukhā caitasikī vedanā sukhā sāmiṣavedanā duḥkhā	cEtasikI vedanA aduHKa-asuKA cEtasikI vedanA suKA sa-Amiza-vedanA duHKA
   sāmiṣavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā sāmiṣavedanā sukhā nirāmiṣavedanā duḥkhā	sa-Amiza-vedanA aduHKa-asuKA sa-Amiza-vedanA suKA nirAmiza-vedanA duHKA
   nirāmiṣavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā nirāmiṣavedanā punaḥ sukhā gredhāśritavedanā	nirAmiza-vedanA aduHKa-asuKA nirAmiza-vedanA punar suKA greDa-ASrita-vedanA
   duḥkhā gredhāśritavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā gredhāśritavedanā sukhā	duHKA greDa-ASrita-vedanA aduHKa-asuKA greDa-ASrita-vedanA suKA
   naiṣkramyāśritavedanā duḥkhā naiṣkramyāśritavedanā aduḥkhāsukhā	nEzkramya-ASrita-vedanA duHKA nEzkramya-ASrita-vedanA aduHKa-asuKA
   naiṣkramyānnitavedanā ca // kāyikī vedanā katamā / paṃcavijñānasaṃprayuktā	nEzkramya-annita-vedanA ca // kAyikI vedanA katamA / paMca-vijQAna-saMprayuktA
   vedanā // caitasikī vedanā katamā / manovijñānasaṃprayuktā vedanā /	vedanA // cEtasikI vedanA katamA / manaH-vijQAna-saMprayuktA vedanA /

   svaparasamayajñatā vākkaraṇasaṃpad vaiśaradyaṃ pratibhānaṃ sthairyaṃ	sva-para-samaya-jQa-tA vAkkaraNa-saMpad vESaradyam pratiBAnam sTEryam
   dākṣiṇyaṃ ca //	dAkziNyam ca //

   anyavastupratisaraṇena vyāvṛttiḥ bāhyavastuvacanena	anya-vastu-pratisaraNena vyAvRttiH bAhya-vastu-vacanena

   sūtre / kathādoṣaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa navavidhaḥ / ākulaṃ saṃrabdham agamakam	sUtre / kaTA-dozaH saMkzepeNa navaviDaH / Akulam saMrabDam agamakam
   amitam anarthakam akālam asthiram apradīptam apravaddhaṃ ca //	amitam anarTakam akAlam asTiram apradIptam apravadDam ca //
   ṣaṣṭhaṃ vādaniḥsaraṇaṃ guṇadoṣau vicārya vādānniḥsaratyakaraṇena vā	zazWam vAda-niHsaraNam guNa-dozO vicArya vAdAt-niHsarati-akaraNena vA
   prativādityabhājanatāṃ parṣado vaiguṇyamātmano 'kauśalyaṃ ca jñātvā vādaṃ	prativAditya-BAjana-tAm parzadaH vEguNyam-AtmanaH akOSalyam ca jQAtvA vAdam
   na karoti / prativādini bhājanatāṃ parṣado guṇavattvamātmanaḥ kauśalyaṃ ca	na karoti / prativAdini BAjana-tAm parzadaH guNavat-tvam-AtmanaH kOSalyam ca
   jñātvā vādaṃ karoti //	jQAtvA vAdam karoti //
   (Abhidh-s 106)	(a-aBiD-H 106)
   vāde bahukarā dharmāḥ samāsatastrayaḥ / svaparasamayajñatā yayā sarvatra	vAde bahu-karAH DarmAH samAsatas-trayaH / sva-para-samaya-jQa-tA yayA sarvatra

   / pratimānaṃ yena nipuṇaḥ sarvāṃn kaṭhinān praśnān vyākaroti //	/ pratimAnam yena nipuNaH sarvAn kaWinAn praSnAn vyAkaroti //

   vivādaṃ kartum / taduktaṃ bhagavatā mahāyānā bhidharmasutre /	vivAdam kartum / tat-uktam BagavatA mahAyAnAH BiDarmasutre /

   saṃpratyayo durlabhaḥ / prāśnikānāmavavādagrāhakaṃ cittaṃ durlabham /	saMpratyayaH durlaBaH / prASnikAnAm-avavAda-grAhakam cittam durlaBam /

   durlabhaḥ / katame ṣaṭ / asatpakṣabhiniveśadoṣaḥ kusṛtivacanadoṣaḥ	durlaBaH / katame zaw / asat-pakza-BiniveSa-dozaH kusRti-vacana-dozaH
   akālikavākkaraṇadoṣaḥ kathāsādadoṣaḥ pārupyavacatadoṣaḥ cittāghātadoṣaśca	akAlika-vAk-karaNa-dozaH kaTA-AsAda-dozaH pArupi-avacata-dozaH citta-AGAta-dozaH-ca
   / vāde saṃrambhābhāvo durlabhaḥ / vāde paracittānurakṣaṇaṃ durlabham /	/ vAde saMramBa-aBAvaH durlaBaH / vAde para-citta-anurakzaNam durlaBam /
   vāde anurakṣaṇe 'pi cittasamādhidurlabhaḥ / vāde cittasya	vAde anurakzaNe api citta-samADi-durlaBaH / vAde cittasya

   'bhāvite tu asamāhicittasya kṣipraṃ samādhilābhaḥ samāhitacittasya vā	aBAvite tu asama-ahi-cittasya kzipram samADi-lABaH samAhita-cittasya vA

   abhisandhiviniścayaḥ katamaḥ / uktādanyo 'rthaḥ / nāmapadavyañjanakāyānāṃ	aBisanDi-viniScayaH katamaH / uktAt-anyaH arTaH / nAma-pada-vyaQjana-kAyAnAm

   (Abhidh-s 107)	(a-aBiD-H 107)
   yathoktaṃ sūtre /	yaTA-uktam sUtre /

   sūtre / bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ pañcadharmasamanvāgato brahmacārī bhavati	sUtre / boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH paQca-Darma-samanvAgataH brahmacArI Bavati

   maithunyānmaithunasya niḥsaraṇaṃ paryeṣate / maithunaprahāṇenopekṣako	mETunyAt-mETunasya niHsaraNam paryezate / mETuna-prahANena-upekzakaH-
